class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><strong><span>D-H参数表</span></strong><span>：</span></p><div class="ds-scroll-area _1210dd7 c03cafe9"><div class="ds-scroll-area__gutters" style="position: sticky; top: 0px; left: 0px; right: 0px; height: 0px; --container-height: 137px;"><div class="ds-scroll-area__horizontal-gutter" style="left: 0px; right: 0px; top: calc(var(--container-height) - 14px); height: 10px;"><div class="ds-scroll-area__horizontal-bar" style="display: none;"></div></div><div class="ds-scroll-area__vertical-gutter" style="right: 0px; top: 8px; bottom: calc(0px - var(--container-height) + 8px); width: 10px;"><div class="ds-scroll-area__vertical-bar" style="display: none;"></div></div></div><table><thead><tr><th><span>连杆</span></th><th><span>aᵢ</span></th><th><span>αᵢ</span></th><th><span>dᵢ</span></th><th><span>θᵢ</span></th></tr></thead><tbody><tr><td><span>1</span></td><td><span>L₁</span></td><td><span>0</span></td><td><span>0</span></td><td><span>θ₁</span></td></tr><tr><td><span>2</span></td><td><span>L₂</span></td><td><span>0</span></td><td><span>0</span></td><td><span>θ₂</span></td></tr></tbody></table></div><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><strong><span>坐标系建立</span></strong><span>：</span></p><ul><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>基坐标系{O₀}：原点在关节1，z₀垂直平面向外</span></p></li><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>坐标系{O₁}：原点在关节2，x₁沿连杆1方向</span></p></li><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>坐标系{O₂}：原点在末端，x₂沿连杆2方向</span></p></li></ul><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>通过这种方法，可以系统地为任何机械臂构型建立完整的坐标系系统。</span></p>

---

### 用户

雅各比矩阵是什么

---

### DeepSeek AI

<p>思考：</p><blockquote><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>雅可比矩阵在机器人学中是一个非常重要的概念，它描述了机器人末端执行器的速度与关节速度之间的关系。具体来说，雅可比矩阵是一个线性变换矩阵，它将关节速度向量映射到末端执行器的线速度和角速度。</span></p><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>在数学上，雅可比矩阵可以表示为：</span></p><span class="katex-display ds-markdown-math"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" display="block"><semantics><mrow><mrow><mo fence="true">[</mo><mtable rowspacing="0.16em" columnalign="center" columnspacing="1em"><mtr><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="false"><mi>v</mi></mstyle></mtd></mtr><mtr><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="false"><mi>ω</mi></mstyle></mtd></mtr></mtable><mo fence="true">]</mo></mrow><mo>=</mo><mi>J</mi><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>q</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mover accent="true"><mi>q</mi><mo>˙</mo></mover></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\begin{bmatrix}
v \\ \omega
\end{bmatrix}
= J(q) \dot{q}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:2.4em;vertical-align:-0.95em;"></span><span class="minner"><span class="mopen delimcenter" style="top:0em;"><span class="delimsizing size3">[</span></span><span class="mord"><span class="mtable"><span class="col-align-c"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:1.45em;"><span style="top:-3.61em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:3em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.03588em;">v</span></span></span><span style="top:-2.41em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:3em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.03588em;">ω</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.95em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose delimcenter" style="top:0em;"><span class="delimsizing size3">]</span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:1em;vertical-align:-0.25em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.09618em;">J</span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.03588em;">q</span><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="mord accent"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.6679em;"><span style="top:-3em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:3em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.03588em;">q</span></span><span style="top:-3em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:3em;"></span><span class="accent-body" style="left:-0.0556em;"><span class="mord">˙</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.1944em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>其中：</span></p><ul><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>v</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">v</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.4306em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.03588em;">v</span></span></span></span><span> 是末端执行器的线速度，</span></p></li><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>ω</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\omega</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.4306em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.03588em;">ω</span></span></span></span><span> 是末端执行器的角速度，</span></p></li><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>J</mi><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>q</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">J(q)</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:1em;vertical-align:-0.25em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.09618em;">J</span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.03588em;">q</span><span class="mclose">)</span></span></span></span><span> 是雅可比矩阵，它是关节位置 </span><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>q</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">q</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.625em;vertical-align:-0.1944em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.03588em;">q</span></span></span></span><span> 的函数，</span></p></li><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mover accent="true"><mi>q</mi><mo>˙</mo></mover></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\dot{q}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.8623em;vertical-align:-0.1944em;"></span><span class="mord accent"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.6679em;"><span style="top:-3em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:3em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.03588em;">q</span></span><span style="top:-3em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:3em;"></span><span class="accent-body" style="left:-0.0556em;"><span class="mord">˙</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.1944em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span> 是关节速度向量。</span></p></li></ul><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>雅可比矩阵通常分为两部分：</span></p><ul><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>上半部分为</span><strong><span>线速度雅可比矩阵</span></strong><span>，记作 </span><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>J</mi><mi>v</mi></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">J_v</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.8333em;vertical-align:-0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.09618em;">J</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.1514em;"><span style="top:-2.55em;margin-left:-0.0962em;margin-right:0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right:0.03588em;">v</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.15em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span>，它关联关节速度与末端线速度。</span></p></li><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>下半部分为</span><strong><span>角速度雅可比矩阵</span></strong><span>，记作 </span><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>J</mi><mi>ω</mi></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">J_\omega</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.8333em;vertical-align:-0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.09618em;">J</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.1514em;"><span style="top:-2.55em;margin-left:-0.0962em;margin-right:0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right:0.03588em;">ω</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.15em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span>，它关联关节速度与末端角速度。</span></p></li></ul><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>因此，雅可比矩阵可以写为：</span></p><span class="katex-display ds-markdown-math"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" display="block"><semantics><mrow><mi>J</mi><mo>=</mo><mrow><mo fence="true">[</mo><mtable rowspacing="0.16em" columnalign="center" columnspacing="1em"><mtr><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="false"><msub><mi>J</mi><mi>v</mi></msub></mstyle></mtd></mtr><mtr><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="false"><msub><mi>J</mi><mi>ω</mi></msub></mstyle></mtd></mtr></mtable><mo fence="true">]</mo></mrow></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">J = \begin{bmatrix}
J_v \\ J_\omega
\end{bmatrix}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.09618em;">J</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:2.4em;vertical-align:-0.95em;"></span><span class="minner"><span class="mopen delimcenter" style="top:0em;"><span class="delimsizing size3">[</span></span><span class="mord"><span class="mtable"><span class="col-align-c"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:1.45em;"><span style="top:-3.61em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:3em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.09618em;">J</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.1514em;"><span style="top:-2.55em;margin-left:-0.0962em;margin-right:0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right:0.03588em;">v</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.15em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="top:-2.41em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:3em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.09618em;">J</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.1514em;"><span style="top:-2.55em;margin-left:-0.0962em;margin-right:0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right:0.03588em;">ω</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.15em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.95em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose delimcenter" style="top:0em;"><span class="delimsizing size3">]</span></span></span></span></span></span></span><h3><span>如何计算雅可比矩阵？</span></h3><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>有两种常见的方法计算雅可比矩阵：</span></p><ol start="1"><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><strong><span>向量积方法</span></strong><span>（Vector Cross Product Method）</span></p></li><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><strong><span>微分变换法</span></strong><span>（Differential Transformation Method）</span></p></li></ol><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>这里我们主要介绍向量积方法，因为它直观且常用。</span></p><h4><span>向量积方法</span></h4><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>对于具有 </span><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>n</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">n</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.4306em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">n</span></span></span></span><span> 个关节的机器人，雅可比矩阵的每一列对应于一个关节对末端速度的贡献。对于第 </span><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>i</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">i</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.6595em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">i</span></span></span></span><span> 个关节：</span></p><ul><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><strong><span>如果关节 </span><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>i</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">i</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.6595em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">i</span></span></span></span><span> 是旋转关节</span></strong><span>：</span></p><ul><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>线速度部分：</span><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>J</mi><mrow><mi>v</mi><mi>i</mi></mrow></msub><mo>=</mo><msub><mi>z</mi><mrow><mi>i</mi><mo>−</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow></msub><mo>×</mo><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msub><mi>p</mi><mrow><mi>e</mi><mi>n</mi><mi>d</mi></mrow></msub><mo>−</mo><msub><mi>p</mi><mrow><mi>i</mi><mo>−</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow></msub><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">J_{vi} = z_{i-1} \times (p_{end} - p_{i-1})</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.8333em;vertical-align:-0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.09618em;">J</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.3117em;"><span style="top:-2.55em;margin-left:-0.0962em;margin-right:0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right:0.03588em;">v</span><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">i</span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.15em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.7917em;vertical-align:-0.2083em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.04398em;">z</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.3117em;"><span style="top:-2.55em;margin-left:-0.044em;margin-right:0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">i</span><span class="mbin mtight">−</span><span class="mord mtight">1</span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.2083em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">×</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:1em;vertical-align:-0.25em;"></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">p</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.3361em;"><span style="top:-2.55em;margin-left:0em;margin-right:0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">e</span><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">n</span><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">d</span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.15em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">−</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:1em;vertical-align:-0.25em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">p</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.3117em;"><span style="top:-2.55em;margin-left:0em;margin-right:0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">i</span><span class="mbin mtight">−</span><span class="mord mtight">1</span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.2083em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose">)</span></span></span></span></p></li><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>角速度部分：</span><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>J</mi><mrow><mi>ω</mi><mi>i</mi></mrow></msub><mo>=</mo><msub><mi>z</mi><mrow><mi>i</mi><mo>−</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">J_{\omega i} = z_{i-1}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.3117em;"><span style="top:-2.55em;margin-left:-0.0962em;margin-right:0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.15em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.3117em;"><span style="top:-2.55em;margin-left:-0.044em;margin-right:0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">i</span><span class="mbin mtight">−</span><span class="mord mtight">1</span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.2083em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p></li></ul></li><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><strong><span>如果关节 </span><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>i</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">i</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.6595em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">i</span></span></span></span><span> 是移动关节</span></strong><span>：</span></p><ul><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>线速度部分：</span><span class="katex"><span vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.3117em;"><span style="top:-2.55em;margin-left:-0.0962em;margin-right:0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right:0.03588em;">v</span><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">i</span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.6389em;vertical-align:-0.2083em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.04398em;">z</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.3117em;"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">i</span><span class="mbin mtight">−</span><span class="mord mtight">1</span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.2083em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p></li><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>角速度部分：</span><span class="katex"><span encoding="application/x-tex">J_{\omega i} = 0</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.8333em;vertical-align:-0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.09618em;">J</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.3117em;"><span style="top:-2.55em;margin-left:-0.0962em;margin-right:0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">ωi</span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.15em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="height:0.6444em;"></span><span class="mord">0</span></span></span></span></p></li></ul></li></ul><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>其中：</span></p><ul><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>z</mi><mrow><mi>i</mi><mo>−</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\begin{bmatrix}
\dot{x} \\ \dot{y}
\end{bmatrix}
=
\begin{bmatrix}
-L_1 \sin\theta_1 - L_2 \sin(\theta_1+\theta_2) &amp; -L_2 \sin(\theta_1+\theta_2) \\
L_1 \cos\theta_1 + L_2 \cos(\theta_1+\theta_2) &amp; L_2 \cos(\theta_1+\theta_2)
\end{bmatrix}
\begin{bmatrix}
\dot{\theta_1} \\ \dot{\theta_2}
\end{bmatrix}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:2.4em;vertical-align:-0.95em;"></span><span style="height:0.15em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">+</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2222em;"></span><span class="mord accent"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.9313em;"><span style="top:-3em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:3em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.02778em;">θ</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.3011em;"><span style="top:-2.55em;margin-left:-0.0278em;margin-right:0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight">2</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.15em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="top:-3.2634em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:3em;"></span><span class="accent-body" class="vlist" style="height:2.05em;"><span style="top:-4.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:5.6em;"></span><span style="width:0.667em;height:3.600em;"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>但通常我们只考虑平面内的角速度，即标量值。在完整的雅可比矩阵中，角速度部分应为三维向量，但这里只有z方向有值。因此，完整的雅可比矩阵（考虑三维）为：</span></p><span class="katex-display ds-markdown-math"><span class="katex"><span stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mstyle></mtd></mtr><mtr><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="false"><mn>0</mn></mstyle></mtd><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" L_1 \cos\theta_1 + L_2 \cos(\theta_1+\theta_2) &amp; L_2 \cos(\theta_1+\theta_2) \\
0 &amp; 0 \\
0 &amp; 0 \\
0 &amp; 0 \\
1 &amp; 1
\end{bmatrix}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.09618em;">J</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:7.2001em;vertical-align:-3.35em;"></span><span class="minner"><span class="mopen"><span class="delimsizing mult"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:3.85em;"><span style="top:-5.8499em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:9.2em;"></span><span style="width:0.667em;height:7.200em;"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="0.667em" height="7.200em" viewBox="0 0 667 7200"><path d="M403 1759 V84 H666 V0 H319 V1759 v3600 v1759 h347 v-84

style="top:-2.55em;margin-left:-0.0278em;margin-right:0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight">2</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.15em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose">)</span></span></span><span style="top:-3.61em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:3em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord">0</span></span></span><span style="top:-2.41em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:3em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord">0</span></span></span><span style="top:-1.21em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:3em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord">0</span></span></span><span style="top:-0.01em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:3em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord">1</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:3.35em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose"><span class="delimsizing mult"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:3.85em;"><span style="top:-5.8499em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:9.2em;"></span><span style="width:0.667em;height:7.200em;"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="0.667em" height="7.200em" viewBox="0 0 667 7200"><path d="M347 1759 V0 H0 V84 H263 V1759 v3600 v1759 H0 v84 H347z
M347 1759 V0 H263 V1759 v3600 v1759 h84z"></path></svg></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:3.35em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>这里，前两行对应线速度的x和y分量，第三、四、五行对应角速度的x、y、z分量。由于是平面运动，角速度只有z方向非零。</span></p><h3><span>雅可比矩阵的用途</span></h3><ol start="1"><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><strong><span>速度映射</span></strong><span>：将关节速度映射到末端执行器的速度。</span></p></li><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><strong><span>静力映射</span></strong><span>：利用雅可比矩阵的转置可以将末端执行器上的力映射到关节力矩（虚功原理）。</span></p></li><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><strong><span>奇异性分析</span></strong><span>：当雅可比矩阵不满秩时，机器人处于奇异位形，此时某些方向的运动无法实现。</span></p></li><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><strong><span>轨迹规划</span></strong><span>：在控制中，雅可比矩阵用于逆运动学求解，以实现末端执行器的期望运动。</span></p></li></ol><h3><span>注意事项</span></h3><ul><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>雅可比矩阵依赖于机器人的当前构型，因此它是随关节位置变化而变化的。</span></p></li><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>在奇异位形时，雅可比矩阵的秩减少，机器人失去某些方向的运动能力，并且逆运动学解可能不存在或不是唯一的。</span></p></li></ul><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>希望这个解释能帮助你理解雅可比矩阵。如果你有具体机械臂的雅可比矩阵计算问题，我可以帮你详细计算。</span></p></blockquote><br/><h2><span>雅可比矩阵详解</span></h2><h3><span>1. 基本概念</span></h3><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><strong><span>雅可比矩阵</span></strong><span>在机器人学中是一个非常重要的数学工具，它描述了机器人</span><strong><span>末端执行器的运动速度</span></strong><span>与</span><strong><span>各个关节运动速度</span></strong><span>之间的映射关系。</span></p><h3><span>2. class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>其中：</span></p><ul><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><strong><span>τ</span></strong><span>：关节力矩向量</span></p></li><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><strong><span>F</span></strong><span>：末端力/力矩向量</span></p></li></ul><h4><span>d) 轨迹规划和控制</span></h4><ul><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>用于计算实现期望末端轨迹所需的关节速度</span></p></li><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>在视觉伺服、力控制等领域广泛应用</span></p></li></ul><h3><span>7. 注意事项</span></h3><ol start="1"><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><strong><span>构型依赖性</span></strong><span>：雅可比矩阵依赖于机械臂的当前构型</span></p></li><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><strong><span>实时计算</span></strong><span>：在实际控制中需要实时计算</span></p></li><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><strong><span>数值稳定性</span></strong><span>：在奇异点附近需要特殊处理</span></p></li><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><strong><span>计算效率</span></strong><span>：对于复杂机械臂，需要优化计算方法</span></p></li></ol><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>雅可比矩阵是机器人运动学、动力学和控制中的核心概念，深入理解它对于机器人系统分析和设计至关重要。</span></p>
